NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

 [Part VI—Sec. 4
PUBLIC   NOTICES
E. Kumaran, a male child, son of Thiru V. Elumalai, born on 23rd June 1990, residing at No. 8020, 46th Cross Street, 
Kannagi Nagar, 195th Ward, Oggiam Thuraipakkam, Chennai-600 097, has been living as a Transwomen. I have been 
Granted Identity  Card No. TG01858, issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and Women Empowerment 
Department.  By this, I may be treated as a Transwomen  and shall henceforth be known as  E. MAYASRI
Chennai,	
	
               E. KUMARAN
9th June 2022.
M. Shanmugam, a male child, son of (late) Thiru Mahali, born on 5th January 1987, residing at No. 6/53C, 
2nd Floor, Pari 1st Cross Street, Choollaimedu, Chennai-600 094, has been living as a Transgenderwomen. I have been 
Granted Identity  Card No. TG02468, issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP 
Department.  By this, I may be treated as a Transgenderwomen  and shall henceforth be known as  M. SHALINI.
Chennai,	
	
               	
M. SHANMUGAM
16th June 2022.
